1a1(phal chen): @#/ /phal chen cha pa bzhugs so//
1b1(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po che las/ sdong
1b2(phal chen): pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/ bam po brgya gcig pa/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang
1b3(phal chen): m tshan mo'i lha mo sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi byang chub sems
1b4(phal chen): d pa'i rnam par thar pa'i 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas 'gro ba rnam par 'dul
2a1(phal chen): ba de la yongs su bsgom zhing khong du chud par bya ba dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / 'jug
2a2(phal chen): par bya ba dang / shin tu rgyas par bya ba dang / yongs su khyab par bya ba dang / rab tu mchod par bya ba dang /
2a3(phal chen): dbang du bya ba dang / snang bar bya ba dang / yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba byed cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya
2a4(phal chen): m tsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa gang na ba der phyin te mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i rkang
2a5(phal chen): p a gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la lan brgya stong
2b1(phal chen): d u mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i mdun du 'dug ste thal mo
2b2(phal chen): sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /'phags ma lha mo/ bdag ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du yang dag
2b3(phal chen): par zhugs pa ste/ bdag ni/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rten gyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la slob cing byang chub sems
2b4(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa la zhugs te byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la nan tan du bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la rab
2b5(phal chen): tu gnas pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung bar 'tshal na/ 'phags ma lha mo/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang
2b6(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol/ de nas mtshan
3a1(phal chen): mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang la 'di skad ces smras so/ /
3a2(phal chen): rigs kyi bu/ de ltar khyod dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rten gyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su tshol ba legs so/ /
3a3(phal chen): legs so/ /rigs kyi bu/ kho mo ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems
3a4(phal chen): kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa thob pa'o/ /nor bzang gis smras pa/ 'phags ma/ khyod ni/ 'phrin las ci mdzad/ yul gang
3a5(phal chen): dang ldan/ sbyor ba gang dang ldan/ ci la rnam par dpyod/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs
3a6(phal chen): 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa de'i yul ni/ ji lta bu zhig mchis/ des smras pa/ rigs kyi bu/ kho mo ni/
3b1(phal chen): sems dang bsam pa rgya mtsho yongs su dag pa'i mnyam pa nyid du zhugs pa ste/ 'jig rten gyi rdul dang dri ma thams cad rnam par bsal ba'i mi phyed pas brgyan
3b2(phal chen): pa'i bsam pa la zhugs pa'o/ /brtsams pa las mi ldog /mi ldog pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /rin po che'i ri bo ltar yon tan gyis brgyan pa'i sems mi sgul
3b3(phal chen): ba dang ldan pa'o/ /mi gnas mi rten pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /'gro ba thams cad yongs su bskyab pa la mngon par phyogs pa'i sems can dang ldan pa'o/ /sangs rgyas rgya mtsho
3b4(phal chen): thams cad mthong bas mi ngoms pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi stobs kyi bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /dran
3b5(phal chen): pa'i rgya mtsho ye shes kyi snang ba chen pos brgyan pa la yang dag par gnas pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o/ /sems can thams cad mya ngan gyi dgon pa las yang dag par
3b6(phal chen): bzla ba la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad sdug bsngal dang / yid mi bde ba las rnam par zlog pa la mngon par brtson pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi yid du mi
3b7(phal chen): 'ong ba'i gzugs dang / sgra dang / dri dang / ro dang / reg yongs su rgyu ba rnam par zlog pa la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi sdug pa dang mi sdug pa dang bral
4a1(phal chen): zhing phrad pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi yul gyi rkyen las byung bas mgo rmongs pa'i sdug bsngal
4a2(phal chen): rnam par zlog pa la rab tu brtson pa'o/ /log par ltung ba'i sems can thams cad kyi rten du gyur pa'o/ /sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i gnas kyi sdug bsngal las
4a3(phal chen): 'byung ba yang dag par ston pa la mngon par brtson pa'o/ /sems can thams cad kyi rga shi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid
4a4(phal chen): mi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa rnam par zlog pa la zhugs pa'o/ /sems can thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba bla na med pa yongs su sgrub par zhugs pa ste/
4a5(phal chen): grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul dang / khams dang / rgyal po'i gnas na 'khod pa'i sems can thams cad bde bar rim gror bya bas nyams dga' bar
4a6(phal chen): 'gyur zhing / de dag la chos dang mthun par bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang / rim gro bya ba yang legs par byed de/ de dag rim pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du
4a7(phal chen): yongs su smin par byed do/ /'di lta ste/ khang khyim dang / gzhal med khang na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyi mngon par chags pa med pa yongs su skyed do/ /yid
4b1(phal chen): mi bde ba de dang de dag kyang rnam par sel to/ /mngon par zhen pa thams cad rgyun gcad pa dang / chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston
4b2(phal chen): to| |pha ma dang / phu nu dang / sring mo dang / gnyen bshes dang / 'grogs pa'i sems can yun ring po nas bshes shing mdza' bar gyur pa dag las sangs rgyas dang
4b3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' dang 'phrad par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bu smad dang 'grogs pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i sred pa thams cad rab tu spang ba dang / sems
4b4(phal chen): can thams cad la mnyam pa nyid kyi sems su bya ba dang / snying rje chen po rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /tshong 'dus kyi dbus na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams
4b5(phal chen): la 'phags pa'i dge 'dun dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong bar bya ba la yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /longs spyod kyi dregs pas myos pa'i
4b6(phal chen): sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /glu dang / gar dang / rol mo la mngon par dga' ba'i sems can rnams
4b7(phal chen): la chos kyi dga' ba la mos par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /yul gyi dga' ba la chags pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la yang dag par gzhol
5a1(phal chen): bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /khro bas yongs su non pa'i sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos
5a2(phal chen): ston to| |sems can le lo can rnams la brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /sems rnam par myos pa'i sems can rnams
5a3(phal chen): la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lta ba'i rnam pa thibs por zhugs pa'i sems can ma rig pa'i
5a4(phal chen): mun nag tu 'thom pa rnams la lta ba'i rnam pa thibs po dang / ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par bsal ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /shes rab 'chal ba can gyi sems can rnams
5a5(phal chen): la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /khams gsum pa la mngon par zhen pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba las 'byung bar
5a6(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /
5a7(phal chen): bdag la phan par brtson pa'i sems can rnams la sems can thams cad la phan par bya ba'i smon lam yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /
5b1(phal chen): bsam pa nyam chung ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /ma rig pa'i mun pas sems blong
5b2(phal chen): ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /gzugs mi sdug pa dang ldan pa'i sems can
5b3(phal chen): rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lus kyi dbyibs mi mdzes pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la chos kyi sku
5b4(phal chen): bla na med pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /kha dog mi sdug pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mdog gser gyi kha dog lta bu dang /
5b5(phal chen): shin tu 'jam zhing ka tsa lin+da ka ltar reg na bde ba'i lus rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /sdug bsngal ba'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde
5b6(phal chen): ba dam pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bde ba'i sems can rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bde ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /nad pa na ba'i
5b7(phal chen): sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i lus gzugs brnyan lta bu yongs su grub par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /dga' ba sna tshogs la brtson pa'i sems can
6a1(phal chen): rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dga' ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /phongs pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems
6a2(phal chen): dpa'i chos kyi gter dang mdzod rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bza' shing gi ra ba na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su btsal
6a3(phal chen): ba la mngon par brtson pa'i rgyu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /lam du zhugs pa'i sems can rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam du 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos
6a4(phal chen): ston to/ /grong na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la khams gsum pa thams cad las 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /yul gyi 'dabs na gnas pa'i sems can
6a5(phal chen): rnams la nyan thos dang rnag byang chub kyi lam las yang dag par 'da' bar bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /grong
6a6(phal chen): rdal na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang du gnas par 'gyur ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /phyogs mtshams na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la dus
6a7(phal chen): gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /phyogs na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la chos thams cad kyi ye shes mngon par shes
6b1(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /'dod chags la gcig tu dga' ba'i sems can rnams la mi sdug pa'i sgos 'khor ba'i sred pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /zhe sdang
6b2(phal chen): la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la byams pa chen po'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /gti mug la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la chos thams cad kyi sgo
6b3(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu 'byed pa'i ye shes mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la theg pa thams cad kyi smon lam gyi tshul
6b4(phal chen): rgya mtshos khyad par du 'gro bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /'khor ba'i yul gyi dga' ba'i bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i yul dga' ba rnam par bzlog
6b5(phal chen): pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis gtses pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis nye bar nyon mongs pa med par
6b6(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mi skye ba'i gnas yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /phung po la gnas pa'i
6b7(phal chen): bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la gzhi med pa'i chos kyi spyod yul la rnam par spyod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /bsam pa zhum pa'i sems can rnams la lam gyi
7a1(phal chen): rgyan gyi khyad par yang dag par bstan par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /mtho ba'i nga rgyal can gyi sems can rnams la chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi
7a2(phal chen): bzod pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos ston to/ /g.yo sgyu'i yul gyi bsam pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongs su dag
7a3(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ /de ltar rigs kyi bu/ kho mo ni/ sems can thams cad chos kyi sbyin pas yongs su bsdus shing ngan song gi lam gyi rgyud sdug bsngal ba
7a4(phal chen): thams cad nas rnam par bzlog pa dang / lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa dang / bde ba yongs su bstan pa dang / khams gsum pa las gyen du bskyed pa dang / thams
7a5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu dgod pa dang / thabs sna tshogs kyis yongs su smin par byed byed pas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho snang ba rab tu thob pas dga' zhing
7a6(phal chen): spro la yid bde bar gyur pa'o/ /gzhan yang rigs kyi bu/ kho mo ni/ phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho la rnam par
7a7(phal chen): lta zhing smon lam rgya mtsho la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' lus sna tshogs rnam par dag pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'od zer dang 'od kyi
7b1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor kha dog mtha' yas pa rab tu 'gyed pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshul rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa'i ye shes snang ba can/ ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs
7b2(phal chen): pa| rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyi yul dang ldan pa/ dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / skad rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi dbyangs dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyis rnam par klubs pa'i lus can/
7b3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ zhing rgya mtsho 'byams klas pa sna tshogs su zhugs pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ tha
7b4(phal chen): dad pa yang dag par shes pa rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / ye shes kyi yul sna tshogs kyis snang bar gyur pa/ ye shes rgya mtsho
7b5(phal chen): sna tshogs kyi snang ba rab tu thob pa/ ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi tshul la rnam par spyod pa/ chos sna tshogs kyi rnam par thar pa'i gzhal med khang rnam par rtse ba'i yul
7b6(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo sna tshogs le mngon du gnas pa/ chos kyi dbyings sna tshogs kyi nam mkha'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis nam mkha'
7b7(phal chen): rgyas par 'gengs pa/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sna tshogs la rnam par lta ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams sna tshogs nas 'dus pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs 'byams
8a1(phal chen): klas par rjes su 'dong ngo / /phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs nas yongs su 'dus pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad pas bkye ba/ de bzhin gshegs
8a2(phal chen): pa tha dad pa'i zhabs kyi drung nas lhags pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs sna tshogs kyi 'khor dang ldan pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bebs pa/ de bzhin
8a3(phal chen): gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos rgya mtsho sna tshogs la rnam pa spyod pa/ ye shes sna tshogs rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ rgyan gyi
8a4(phal chen): snying po sna tshogs can gyi stan la 'khod pa rnams kyi dga' ba sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongs su bskyed de/ de dag dga' ba sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongs
8a5(phal chen): su skyes nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshor 'dong ste/ de dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs tshad med pa rjes su sems pas kyang dga'
8a6(phal chen): ba'i shugs chen po rgya mtsho yongs su 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang kho mo ni/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi gzugs kyi sku yongs su
8a7(phal chen): dag pa mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po dang / mos shing nyams bde ba rab tu 'thob ste/ sems kyi skad cig re re
8b1(phal chen): la'ang 'od kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings ltar yangs pa/ kha dog rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med par snang ba la lta zhing / sems kyi skad cig re re la dga' ba chen po'i
8b2(phal chen): shugs rgya mtsho rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang 'od zer chen po sangs rgya kyi zhing
8b3(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste/ 'od zer re re zhing yang 'od zer rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor
8b4(phal chen): dang ldan pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar mdzad pa mthong zhing sems kyi skad cig re re
8b5(phal chen): la dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi dbu dang / sku phrag pa gnyis kyi lhun las
8b6(phal chen): sems kyi skad cig re re la rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i ri'i sprin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung zhing chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho thams
8b7(phal chen): cad rgyas par 'gengs pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad
9a1(phal chen): kyi sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas sems kyis skad cig re re la kha dog dri zhim po dang / 'od zer sna tshogs can gyi sprin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi
9a2(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung zhing sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /
9a3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/ sems kyi skad cig re re la mtshan re re nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku
9a4(phal chen): gzugs mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa'i sprin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad rgyas par 'gengs
9a5(phal chen): pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam pa snang mdzad kyi sku'i dpe byad bzang
9a6(phal chen): po re re las sems kyi skad cig re re la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku dpe byad bzang po brgyad cus shin tu 'bar ba'i sprin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul
9a7(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i dbyangs su sgrog pa'i 'brug
9b1(phal chen): sgra 'byin pa mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la
9b2(phal chen): rnam par bltas nas/ sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa'i sku dang po byang chub tu thugs bskyed pa dang bcas/ pha rol tu
9b3(phal chen): phyin pa'i lam rnam par dag pa'i rgyan dang bcas/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su gnon pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i
9b4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung ba mthong nas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par

15b1(phal chen): do| |de'i dbus na 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che thams cad kyi sprin sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi 'og gi mtshams nas rin po che thams cad kyi phreng ba'i dra ba rgya mtshos

15b7(phal chen): der kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa de mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa mthong nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ /de
16a1(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa de mthong nas kyang kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho'i 'od ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo/ /de'i 'og tu 'jig
16a2(phal chen): r ten gyi khams de nyid kyi rgyal po'i gnas kun nas yongs su rgyas pa'i dpal gyi snying po zhes bya bar snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sdong po ri bo gzi
16a3(phal chen): brjid ces bya ba mngon par sangs rgyas so/ /kho mos ni/ de nas shi 'phos te snying po byang chub de nyid du ye shes phun sum tshogs pa'i bsod nams 'od ces bya ba'i mtshan
16a4(phal chen): mo'i lha mo zhig tu gyur cing 'dug 'dug ste/ kho mos der bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sdong po ri bo gzi brjid des chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i rnam
16a5(phal chen): par 'phrul pa mthong nas 'gro ba thams cad du yongs su ston pa'i mnyam pa nyid kyi 'od kyi yul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo/ /de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de
16a6(phal chen): nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgya mtsho thams cad kyi gsung gi rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu chos thams cad kyi yang
16a7(phal chen): dag par 'phel bar byed pa'i gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo/ /de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa rin po che'i 'od zer sgron ma'i
16b1(phal chen): rgyal mtshan rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu kho mos sangs rgyas rgya mtsho rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo/ /
16b2(phal chen): de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sprin sgra'i rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu
16b3(phal chen): kho mos chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo/ /de'i 'og tu kho mo lha'i bu mo zhig tu gyur te snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs
16b4(phal chen): pa ye shes skar mda' snang ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu kho mos sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi

24a3(phal chen): yas las rnams yongs su 'byung / /'jig rten thams cad las kyis rnam par bris/ /'gro ba sems kyi dngos su mkhyen gyur pas/ /rang gi sku yang 'gro ba snyed du
24a4(phal chen): bstan| |'jig rten du ni rmi lam 'drar mkhyen nas/ /sangs rgyas kun kyang gzugs brnyan lta bu dang / /ma lus chos rnams sgra brnyan 'drar mkhyen pas/ /chags
24a5(phal chen): pa mi mnga' 'gro ba kun tu spyod/ /dus gsum gnas pa'i 'gro ba thams cad la/ /skad cig re rer rang gi sku ston kyang / /khyod kyi thugs la gnyis su mi rgyu ste/ /phyogs
24a6(phal chen): rnams kun tu chos kyang rab tu bstan/ /rdul la 'gro ba rgya mtsho mtha' yas dang / /de bzhin sems can mtsho chen dpag yas dang / /mtha' dbus med pa'i bde
24a7(phal chen): gshegs gang chen mtsho/ /kun kyang khyod kyi rnam thar dam pa'i yul/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang gis mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la
24b1(phal chen): t shul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa de dag gis mngon par bstod de lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te mtshan mo'i lha mo
24b2(phal chen): sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i drung nas song ngo / /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste// ! //bam po
24b3(phal chen): brgya gnyis pa/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa de
24b4(phal chen): ni| sgom pa dang / rjes su sgom pa dang / yang dag par sgom pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i gdams ngag rjes su bstan pa la ni/ rjes su
24b5(phal chen): 'brang bar bya ba dang / rjes su dran par bya ba dang / khong du chud par byed/ tshig dang yi ge re re la ni/ tshul du ma dang bsam pa tshad med pas chos nyid kyi tshul shes pa rjes
24b6(phal chen): su dran par byed cing / dren pas rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / blo gros kyis rnam par dbye ba dang / rigs pas khong du chud par bya ba dang / blos shin tu yangs par bya ba dang /
24b7(phal chen): lus kyis reg par byas te rnam par spyad pa dang / rjes su 'jug pa byed cing / mthar gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gang
25a1(phal chen): na ba der phyin pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal pad+mo'i khri chen po nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po grong
25a2(phal chen): khyer dang / gnas thams cad rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po can la phyogs thams cad dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mngon du gyur pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad
25a3(phal chen): kyi gzugs dang mnyam pa'i lus dang / sems can thams cad la mngon du gyur pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyis ma gos pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams
25a4(phal chen): cad dang rang bzhin mnyam pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba
25a5(phal chen): la mthun pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sgra rab tu sgrog pa'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad du 'pho ba med pa'i lus dang / sgrib pa thams cad shin tu bcom
25a6(phal chen): pa'i lus dang / de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad gdul ba mthar phyin par byed pa'i lus su 'dug cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo brjod du med
25a7(phal chen): p a'i 'khor gyis bskor te 'dug pa mthong nas dga' rangs te mgu zhing nyams bde la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba
25b1(phal chen): ' byung ba'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su
25b2(phal chen): bskor ba byas nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi mdun du 'dug ste thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /lha mo/ /
25b3(phal chen): bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs na/ lha mo/ /ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la rjes su bslab na
25b4(phal chen): sems can la sman par 'gyur ba lags/ ji ltar na/ sems can bla na med pa yongs su bsdu bas yongs su sdud par 'gyur/ ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin
25b5(phal chen): gshegs pas gnang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i las la brtson pa lags/ ji ltar brtson par bgyis na/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi rgyal por nye bar 'gyur ba
25b6(phal chen): bdag la bshad du gsol/ de skad ces smras pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyis tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang la
25b7(phal chen): 'di skad ces smras so/ /rigs kyi bu/ khyod de ltar 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / rnam par gdul ba'i mthar phyin par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
26a1(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par bzung ba'i sbyor ba mthar phyin par bya ba dang / phyogs 'byams klas pa thams cad rgyas par dgang ba'i ye
26a2(phal chen): shes rab tu sbyar ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa mngon du 'gyur ba dang / shes bya nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa mtha' yas
26a3(phal chen): pa rgyas par dgang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu blang zhing yongs su gzung ba'i phyir 'gro ba rgya mtsho thams cad kyi bsam pa ji
26a4(phal chen): lta ba bzhin du chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa'i spyod pa'i tshul yongs su 'dri ba legs so/ /legs so/ /rigs kyi bu/ kho mo ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i
26a5(phal chen): rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'grul ba zab mo la 'jug pa thob pa ste/ de ltar kho mo rnam par thar pa de dang ldan pas chos smra ba chen po'i go 'phang
26a6(phal chen): thogs pa med pa la dmigs pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi mdzod yongs su btang ba'i smon lam dang ldan pa/ snying rje chen po
26a7(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ byams pa chen po'i stobs rab tu thob pa/ sems can thams cad byang chub kyi sems la dgod pa'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba la zhugs
26b1(phal chen): pa| byang chub kyi sems kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / tshogs rab tu bsags pa rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad kha lo sgyur ba'i sa la yang dag par gnas pa/ sems
26b2(phal chen): c an thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi lam la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir 'jig rten gyi chos kyi sprin thams cad las chos kyi nyi ma yongs su dbyung ba'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa
26b3(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bskyed pas 'jig rten thams cad snang bar bya ba'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa'i sems su 'jug pa rgyun mi 'chad pa/ 'gro ba thams
26b4(phal chen): cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'du bya ba yongs su sgrub pa'i sbyor ba shes par bya ba'i phyir sems rnam par dag pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i las kyi lam thams
26b5(phal chen): cad mthun par sgrub pas sems can thams cad kyi ded dpon du zhugs pa/ mi dge ba'i las kyi lam thams cad rab tu spangs pa/ sems can thams cad dge ba'i chos
26b6(phal chen): la rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la lam bde ba yongs su ston pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi theg pa'i rgyan gyi thog
26b7(phal chen): mar 'dren pa la zhugs pa/ dge ba'i chos kyi spyod pa thams cad la sems can thams cad rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad la mi
27a1(phal chen): phyed par bsnyen bkur dang rim gro byed pa la zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba
27a2(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ chos kyi sbyin pa'i sngon 'den cing chos dkar po thams cad yang dag par brtsams pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed
27a3(phal chen): pas mngon par byung bas bsam pa brten zhing mi shigs pa/ rdo rje mthu bo che ltar brtan zhing sra bas sangs rgyas kyi stobs la dmigs pa'i sems rgya chen po'i dkyil
27a4(phal chen): 'khor dang ldan par dge ba'i bshes gnyen la brten cing rnam par spyod de/ kho mo ni/ nyon mongs pa dang / las kyi sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par gtor ba'i
27a5(phal chen): sems dang ldan pa'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs yang dag par rtsom pa'o/ /dkar po'i chos thams cad yang dag par sgrub pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa'o/ /thams
27a6(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid mtha' dang dbus med pa la mngon par 'dun cing dmigs pa'i sems kyi sbyor ba la brtson pa'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de ltar kho mo chos snang ba'i sgo
27a7(phal chen): s ems can thams cad la yongs su ston pa rnam pa de lta bu yongs su sbyong zhing dge pa'i rtsa ba bsags pa'i tshogs la sta gon du gnas pas rnam pa bcus chos kyi
27b1(phal chen): dbyings la rnam par lta zhing khong du chud pa dang / rjes su gzhal bar byed do/ /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ ye shes snang ba shin tu yangs pa thob pas chos kyi dbyings ni/ tshad
27b2(phal chen): med pa khong du chung par byed do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul ba rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ mtha' dang dbus med par
27b3(phal chen): khong du chud par byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su gnan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mchod cing rim gror bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ mu med par khong
27b4(phal chen): du chud par byed do/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ sa mtshams med par khong du
27b5(phal chen): chud par byed do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tha mi dad pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ ris tshad med par khong du chud par byed do/ /
27b6(phal chen): bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can thams cad kyis rnam par dmigs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings
27b7(phal chen): ni/ rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur par khong du chud par byed do/ /'gro ba thams cad rnam par gdul ba'i mthar phyin pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi smon lam gyi mtha
28a1(phal chen): thug pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ rang bzhin gyis rgya che bar khong du chud par byed do/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang
28a2(phal chen): po'i spyod pa 'byams klas pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du gyur par khong du chud par byed do/ /kun tu bzang po'i
28a3(phal chen): spyod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ rgyan gcig tu gyur par khong du chud par byed do/ /dge ba thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings
28a4(phal chen): rgyas par dgang zhing rnam par dag par bya ba chud mi za ba'i chos can du bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni/ thug pa med par khong du chud par byed do/ /rigs kyi bu/ de ltar
28a5(phal chen): kho mo rnam pa bcu po de dag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / tshogs thams cad yongs su bsags pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid la 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs
28a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa rjes su rtogs par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings thams cad la rnam par blta'o/ /khong du chud pa dang / rjes su gzhol bar byed
28a7(phal chen): do| |rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang kho mo de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag nyid che ba nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i yid la bya ba dang ldan pas gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor
28b1(phal chen): gyi rgyud stong phrag bcus sems can rnams la chos ston te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos rgya mtsho thams cad yang dag par 'du ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /
28b2(phal chen): chos thams cad byin gyis rlob pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos kyi sprin thams cad yongs su 'dzin pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / de bzhin gshegs pa
28b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi dgongs pa sgron ma'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /
28b4(phal chen): theg pa'i tshul rgya mtsho dri ma med pa thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgron ma'i snying po'i gzungs
28b5(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo'i glong rab tu sgrog pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi sngon gyi
28b6(phal chen): smon lam rgya mtsho bstan pa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos thams cad la mngon par 'khyil ba'i shugs drag po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor
28b7(phal chen): dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shugs rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / rigs kyi bu/ gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor bcu po de dag la sogs pa
29a1(phal chen): gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud stong phrag bcus sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang kho mo ni/ thos pa'i shes rab kyis
29a2(phal chen): sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /bsam pa'i shes rab dang / bsgoms pa'i shes rab kyis sems can rnams la chos ston te/ srid pa'i rgyud gcig las kyang brtsams
29a3(phal chen): shing sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /srid pa'i rgyud rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang brtsams shing sems can rnams la chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig
29a4(phal chen): gi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos
29a5(phal chen): ston to| |'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /sangs
29a6(phal chen): rgyas gcig gis lung bstan pa las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis lung bstan pa rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston
29a7(phal chen): to| |de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil
29b1(phal chen): 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi 'khor lo las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa
29b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /mdo sde gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi

29b4(phal chen): las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dus pa rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /thams
29b5(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /byang chub kyi sems kyi yan lag rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /theg pa
29b6(phal chen): gcig las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /theg pa thams cad kyi 'byung ba rgya mtsho las kyang brtsams shing chos ston to/ /rigs kyi bu/ de ltar kho mos bstan pa'i tshul
29b7(phal chen): mngon par sgrub pa brjod du med pas sems can rnams la chos ston te/ rigs kyi bu/ de ltar kho mo chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul tha mi dad pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtsho la
30a1(phal chen): 'jug cing sems can thams cad la chos ston pas bla na med pa'i yongs su bsdu ba byed cing / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la phyi
30a2(phal chen): ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa rgya mtshor gnas par bya bas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa
30a3(phal chen): 'di la sems kyi skad cig re re zhing rnam par 'phel ba'i rnam par thar pa'i yul sgom pa'i tshul gyis yongs su sgom ste/ rnam par thar pa'i yul sgom pa'i tshul re
30a4(phal chen): res kyang sems kyi skad cig re re la chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs so/ /nor bzang gis smras pa/ lha mo/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa de
30a5(phal chen): de ltar zab pa ngo mtshar chen/ 'phags ma/ khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa 'di brnyes nas ji srid cig lags/ smras pa/ rigs kyi bu/ sngon 'das
30a6(phal chen): p a'i dus bskal ba 'jig rten gyi rgyud kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol cig tu 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i grong khyer dpal gyi sprin ces bya
30a7(phal chen): ba rin po che'i spos thams cad dang ldan pa/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sprin la blangs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi
30b1(phal chen): smon lam dbyangs su sgrog pa'i pad+mos mtshams rnam par brgyan pa/ lhun sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtshos byung ba'i nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po rgya mtsho las grub
30b2(phal chen): pa/ pad+mo chen po'i dbyibs su 'dug pa/ rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa/ me tog gi khor yug ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor ba/ spos kyi
30b3(phal chen): rin po che ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan ri rab ltar mngon par 'phags pa dang ldan pa/ gling bzhi pa chen po ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ gling
30b4(phal chen): bzhi pa re re zhing yang grong rdal bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang ldan pa byung ngo / /rigs kyi bu/ 'jig rten gyi khams de'i bskal pa mdog dri
30b5(phal chen): ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba byung ste/ bskal pa de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ngo / /'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i grong khyer dpal
30b6(phal chen): gyi sprin gyi gling bzhi pa dbu ma rgyal mtshan sna tshogs zhes bya ba byung ste/ de'i dbus na rgyal po'i gnas rin chan me tog kun tu snang ba zhes bya ba yod par gyur te/ rgyal po'i
30b7(phal chen): gnas de dang ha cang yang mi ring ba zhig na snying po byang chub chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba yod de/ snying po byang chub de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi
31a1(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag gi bskal pa'i dang po la de bzhin gshegs pa chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs 'od kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba byung ste/ d
31a2(phal chen): e'i tshe 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po nyi ma ltar bzhin mdog dri ma med pa zhes bya ba byung nas des bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa chos rgya mtsho thams cad
31a3(phal chen): kyi dbyangs 'od kyi rgyal po las mdo sde chos thams cad kyi glong rgya mtsho zhes bya ba yongs su bzung ste/ bzung nas kyang chos kyi 'khor lo rjes su bskor to/ /yongs su mya
31a4(phal chen): ngan las 'das nas kyang rab tu byung ste bstan pa yongs su bzung ngo / /bstan pa nub tu cha ste/ bstan pa yang stong du gyes/ chos bstan pa shin tu bstan pa'i tshul ni/ brgya
31a5(phal chen): phrag bcur gyur/ rnyog pa'i bskal pa bar ma ni/ nye bar gnas par gyur pa'i che sems can las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pas bsgribs pa/ 'thab mo dang / rtsod pa
31a6(phal chen): dang / dkrugs ma la zhugs par gyur pa dang / dge slong sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i yon tan don du mi gnyer cing yul gyi dga' ba lhur len par gyur pa/ rgyal po dang

38a7(phal chen): sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'jig rten gyi tshig kyal ba rnam par zlog pa/ gnyis su smra ba med pa la rab tu 'god pa/ bden pa la rab
38b1(phal chen): tu gzhog pa'i mthar phyin pa 'di shes par zad na/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa' dag gi lam gyi rang bzhin thams cad thogs pa med par shes pa/ sems kyi skad cig
38b2(phal chen): re re la chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar dbang bsgyur ba/ sems can thams cad kyi sgra skad dang tshig rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ skad rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par 'du
38b3(phal chen): bya ba la mkhas pa/ chos thams cad kyi grangs dang / ming rgya mtsho'i tshul dang chog la mkhas pa/ chos thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs rgya mtsho la dbang
38b4(phal chen): bsgyur ba/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi sprin mngon par sgrub pa la mkhas pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang gdul
38b5(phal chen): bar spyod pa'i mthar phyin par byed pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod pa'am/ sems can thams cad yongs su sdud pa'i nan tan shes par bya ba'am/ byang
38b6(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i lam bla na med par brtsams pa'i sbyor ba'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes shin tu phra ba khong du chud pa'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi gter dang /
38b7(phal chen): mdzod rnam par 'byed pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi gtam la seng+ge'i khri yongs su gnan par bya ba shes par nus re ska na/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/
39a1(phal chen): skyes bu dam pa de dag ni/ chos thams cad kyi sa'i dkyil 'khor gyi gzungs yongs su gnon pa sha stag go /song rigs kyi bu/ bcom ldan 'das rnam
39a2(phal chen): par snang mdzad kyi zhabs kyi drung 'di nyid du mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa zhes bya ba 'dug ste/ kho mo dang rgyang mi ring ba zhig na 'dug
39a3(phal chen): gi / de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa dang / ji ltar nan tan du byed cing / sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen
39a4(phal chen): pa nyid du 'god par byed pa dris shig / de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyis de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa
39a5(phal chen): sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul ba zab mo la 'jug pa 'di nyid brnan te bstan pa'i phyir tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ rnam thar gang gis
39a6(phal chen): dus gsum rgyal ba ma lus dang / /chos dbyings kun tu 'byams klas mtha' dang dbus med pa/ /shes byed mtshan nyid kun gyi gzhir thug rtogs pa yi/ /rgyal sras rnams
39a7(phal chen): kyi rnam thar zab cing blta bar dka'/ /tshogs las byung ba'i rnam thar tshul ni mtha' yas te/ /chos nyid thob pas tshad med bsam du med pa yin/ /yongs su 'phel zhing
39b1(phal chen): kun tu chags med shugs drag par/ /dus gsum byams pa'i tshul gyi lam la 'jug par gyis/ /'di ltar sangs rgyas zhing rgyud rdul phran rab snyed kyi/ /bskal pa 'das
39b2(phal chen): pa'i snga rol sngon gyi zhing byung ba/ /'jig rten khams ni chos 'od sprin gyi grong khyer dpal/ /bskal pa byung ba dri med mdog tu 'od chen no/ /bskal pa de gcig rgyal ba'i
39b3(phal chen): gdung ni rgyud ma chad/ /sangs rgyas ri rab rdul phran rab snyed byung bar gyur/ /bde gshegs chos kyi rgya mtsho 'od dbyangs rgyal po ni/ /thog mar byung ste de dag bskal pa dang po
39b4(phal chen): pa| |rgyal ba chos sprin grong khyer 'od snang rgyal po ni/ /bde gshegs de dag kun gyi tha mar 'jig rten byung / /de dag kun gyi spyan sngar phyin te kho mos mchod/ /de dag kun las
39b5(phal chen): chos kyang dga' ba chen pos thos/ /kho mos thog mar mthong ba gser mdog 'od mnga' ba/ /rgya mtsho'i chos 'od sgrog pa'i gsung gi rgyal po ste/ /mtshan rab sum cu gnyis
39b6(phal chen): kyis yongs brgyan ri bo 'dra/ /mthong nas bdag ni bde gshegs 'gyur snyam blo gros gyur/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de ni kho mos mthong mod la/ /thams cad mkhyen nyid 'byams
39b7(phal chen): klas 'byung ba'i rgyu rkyen gyis/ /mkha' dbyings rnam yangs de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin can/ /rgyal ba'i sems kyi dang po stobs ldan rab tu skyes/ /snying rje bdud rtsi rgya mtsho che las
40a1(phal chen): byung ba des/ /dus gsum gshegs pa'i bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kun/ /rgyal sras rgya mtshos bskor ba ma lus thams cad dang / /sems
40a2(phal chen): can rgya mtshor bcas pa'i rgya mtsho'i zhing yang rgyas/ /lus kyis zhing rnams thams cad ma lus khyab bya dang / /'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa bzhin du lus bstan phyir/ /zhing
40a3(phal chen): rnams ma lus bskyod cing snang bar bya ba dang / /'gro ba smin bya'i don du bdag gis sems kyang bskyed/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa'i spyan sngar kho mo phyin nas kyang / /zhing rnams rgya
40a4(phal chen): mtsho bcu bzhugs rgyal ba'i dbang po mthong / /rgyal ba tha ma mthong nas zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams/ /rgya mtsho'i zhing gi rdul phran rab snyed bzhugs pa mthong / /de yi tshu rol bskal
40a5(phal chen): pa zhing rgyud rdul snyed du/ /rgyal ba 'gro ba'i sgron ma ji snyed skyes gyur pa/ /de dag thams cad spyan sngar kho mo phyin gyur te/ /rnam thar rgya mtsho'i tshul 'di sbyong tshe mchod pa byas//
40a6(phal chen): de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa thob pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo rgya mtsho
40a7(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pa/ gzungs kyi sgo rgya mtsho rgya chen po las byung ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa'i snang ba chen po
40b1(phal chen): rab tu thob pa/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa chen po rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rnam par 'phel ba'i sems dang ldan pa nges mtshan
40b2(phal chen): mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la tshul dang mthun pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do/ /khyod kyi shes rab chos yangs
40b3(phal chen): rgya mtsho kun la spyod/ /srid pa'i rgya mtsho mtha' dbus med par khyod kyis spyad/ /ye shes lus mchog snying po tshe ring snyun bral ba/ /lha mo khyod ni 'khor 'dir byon cing rnam par
40b4(phal chen): mdzes| |chos kyi rang bzhin nam mkha' lta bur thugs chud de/ /dus gsum kun gyi tshul yang chags med thugs chud mdzad/ /thugs kyi skad cig gcig la tshad med bsam
40b5(phal chen): yas pa'i/ /dmigs pa thams cad rtog pa mi mngar 'jal ba mdzad/ /ye shes spyan mnga' chos nyid sems can med gzigs kyang / /sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas thugs
40b6(phal chen): rjes gzigs pa mdzad/ /thugs kyi rnam thar shin tu yangs la 'jug mdzad cing / /sems can tshad med 'dul zhing yongs su smin par mdzad/ /khyod ni chos kyi dkyil 'khor rnam
40b7(phal chen): dpyad tshul mkhyen te/ /chos kyi rang bzhin shes bya'i tshul la rnam sangs rgyas/ /'phags lam dri ma med pa thams cad yongs bsgoms te/ /'gro ba ma lus rnam par sbyong zhing
41a1(phal chen): yongs su 'byung / /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dri med rtogs mdzad pas/ /khyod ni sems can rgya mtsho'i mchog las mngon par skyes/ /khyod ni
41a2(phal chen): chos dbyings khong chud sems can kun khyab par/ /chos rab bstan cing 'jig rten 'jigs pa zhi bar mdzad/ /khyod ni rnam par snang mdzad smon lam lam tshul gyis/ /yang
41a3(phal chen): dag bzhud cing chags med blo yangs dri med ldan/ /thams cad bgod pa'i rgyal ba'i stobs ni thugs chud cing / /zhing rnams kun gyi rgyal ba rnam par 'phrul pa gzigs/ /
41a4(phal chen): khyod kyi thugs ni mkha' 'dra thub par dka' ba ste/ /nyon mongs kun gyi dri mas ma gos snga nas dag /der ni dus gsum byung ba'i zhing rnams thams cad dang / /sangs rgyas sras
41a5(phal chen): dang bcas pa sems can kun bcas 'dus/ /skad cig gcig gis nyin mtshan yud du zla ba dang / /skad cig yud tsam lo dang 'du 'jig bskal pa dang / /bskal pa rgya
41a6(phal chen): mtsho ming grangs rgya mtshor bcas pa dang / /'gro ba rnams kyi 'du shes rgya mtsho'ang thugs su chud/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi sems can skye 'chi ji snyed dang / /gzugs yod
41a7(phal chen): pa dang gzugs med 'du shes yod med kyi/ /rnam spyod bden pa'i tshul ni thugs su chud mdzad cing / /de dag lam bstan byang chub mchog tu 'god pa mdzad/ /rnam par
41b1(phal chen): snang mdzad smon lam dra ba'i rigs las byung / /bde gshegs kun gyi sku gcig tshul las yang dag 'khrungs/ /khyod ni chos sku yongs dag thugs la chags mi mnga'/ /
41b2(phal chen): 'jig rten kun tu sku gzugs yid bzhin ston pa mdzad/ /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang gis mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal
41b3(phal chen): la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigs su bcad pa de dag gis mngon par bstod de/ mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi rkang pa gnyis la
41b4(phal chen): s pyi bos phyag 'tshal nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te yang dang yang
41b5(phal chen): bltas nas mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad srung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi drung nas song ngo / /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya
41b6(phal chen): ba las| sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/ bam po brgya gsum pa/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang / rnam par
41b7(phal chen): 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa de/ de bas kyang rgya cher sgom pa dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / shin tu rgyas par byed cing / mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas
42a1(phal chen): p as bde bar gnas pa gang na ba der phyin nas mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa spos rin po che thams cad kyi
42a2(phal chen): shing gi yal ga'i khang pa brtsegs pa zhig na seng+ge'i khri rin po che'i shing gi myu gu'i snying po can zhig la 'dug ste/ mtshan mo'i lha mo stong phrag bcus kun nas bskor
42a3(phal chen): cing 'dug pa mthong ngo / /de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang gis mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pa'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos
42a4(phal chen): phyag 'tshal te mdun du 'dug nas thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so/ /lha mo/ bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/
42a5(phal chen): ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa dang / ji ltar slob pa dang / ji ltar spyod ji ltar slob cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung ba
42a6(phal chen): bdag la bshad du gsol/ de skad ces smras pa dang / mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang la 'di skad
42a7(phal chen): ces smras so/ /rigs kyi bu/ kho mo'i mthus ni/ mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma nub tu cha ba'i tshe pad+mo shin tu rgyas pa rnams kyang rnam par 'dzum par 'gyur ro//
42b1(phal chen): skyes pa dang bud med bza' shing gi ra ba na gnas shing dga' bar rtse ba la brtson pa dag kyang khyim du 'dong pa'i blo skyed do/ /lam dang srang na rgyu ba'i sems can rnams kyang zhag
42b2(phal chen): gi gnas sems shing tshol te/ 'gro ba'i gnas thams cad du mngon par gzhol bar 'gyur ro/ /nags tshal dang / gseb dang / phug la brten pa'i sems can rnams kyang
42b3(phal chen): nags tshal dang / gseb dang / phug tu 'dong ngo / /shing la gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang shing gi gnas la brten par mngon par gzhol lo/ /khung na gnas pa'i sems
42b4(phal chen): can rnams kyang khung du 'dong ngo / /grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul la gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / yul du 'dong ngo //
42b5(phal chen): chu na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyang chur 'dong ngo / /phyogs gzhan gyi yul du phyin pa'i sems can rnams kyang nub mo bde zhing dga' bar gnas pa'i don du rang rang gi yul
42b6(phal chen): gyi phyogs kyi bsam pa skyed do/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang kho mo ni/ skyes pa dang / bud med gzhon nu dar la bab pa/ dar ba'i nyams drod kyis myos pa dang / glu dang / gar dang /
42b7(phal chen): rol mo'i dga' bas myos pa dang / 'dod pa'i yon tan la dga' zhing brtson pa rnams la skye ba dang / rga shi dang / gti mug gi mun pa chen pos 'jigs pa'i gnyen por dag
43a1(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bskyed pa'i phyir brtson 'grus kyi legs pa'i bsngags pa byed do/ /sems can ser sna dang ldan pa rnams ni/ sbyin pa la
43a2(phal chen): rab tu sbyor ro/ /sems can tshul khrims ngan pa can rnams ni/ tshul khrims la rab tu 'god do/ /ngan sems dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la ni/ byams pa'i
43a3(phal chen): legs pa rjod par byed do/ /sems 'khrugs pa'i sems can rnams ni/ bzod pa la rab tu 'god do/ /le lo can gyi sems can rnams ni/ byang chub sems
43a4(phal chen): dpa'i brtson 'grus brtsam pa la rab tu 'god do/ /sems rnam par myos pa'i sems can rnams ni/ bsam gtan la rab tu 'god do/ /shes rab 'chal ba can gyi
43a5(phal chen): sems can rnams ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yongs su sbyor ro/ /theg pa dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can rnams ni/ theg pa chen po la rab tu 'god do/ /
43a6(phal chen): khams gsum la mngon par zhen pa'i sems can rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa srid pa'i lam gyi rgyud mthar phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor
43a7(phal chen): la spyod pa la rab tu 'god do/ /dmigs pa'i dbang du gyur pa'i sems can las dang nyon mongs pas rab tu mnar ba/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi stobs med pa rnams
43b1(phal chen): ni| byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'god do/ /mi shes pa'i mun nag gis khebs pa'i sems can bdag tu bya ba dang / bdag gir bya bas
43b2(phal chen): ma rig pa'i mun nag tu 'thom pa rnams ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'god do/ /rigs kyi bu/ gzhan yang kho mo ni/ byang chub
43b3(phal chen): sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba'i 'od spro ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba thob pa'o/ /nor bzang gis smras pa/ lha mo/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa
43b4(phal chen): dga' ba'i 'od spro ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba de'i yul ji lta bu zhig mchis/ smras pa/ rigs kyi bu/ rnam par thar pa de ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams
43b5(phal chen): kyis sems can yongs su sdud pa'i ye shes dang thabs snang ba dang ldan pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ sems can rnams kyi bde ba nyams su myong ba ji snyed cig
43b6(phal chen): yod pa de dag thams cad ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams kyi mthus byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdams ngag gi tshul gyis byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs
43b7(phal chen): pa'i gsung la nan tan du byas pas byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su bslab pas byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis byung ba'o/ /de bzhin
44a1(phal chen): gshegs pas bstan pa'i lam la nan tan du byas pas byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dang tshul 'dra ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pas byung ba'o/ /de
44a2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pas chos bstan pa'i mthun pa'i rgyus byung ba'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi nyi ma snang bas byung ba'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
44a3(phal chen): rigs kyi chos dkar po'i dkyil 'khor gyi snang bas ni/ sems can rnams kyi bde ba yongs su 'byung ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar rigs kyi bu/ kho mos byang chub
44a4(phal chen): s ems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba'i 'od spro ba yangs pa yang dag par 'byung ba 'di la 'jug pa'i tshe bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
44a5(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho rjes su dran par byed cing / 'jug pa dang khong du chud par byed pa'i
44a6(phal chen): tshe 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das sngon byang chub sems dpa'i sa la bzhugs pas sems can bdag tu bya ba dang / bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ ma rig pa'i
44a7(phal chen): mun pas 'thom pa/ lta ba thibs po'i lta bas dgon par 'khyams pa/ sred pa'i dbang du gyur pa/ 'dod chags kyi bcings pas glags pa/ zhe sdang gis khong khro
44b1(phal chen): ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ gti mug gis sems kyi rgyud 'khrugs par gyur pa/ phrag dog dang ser sna kun nas 'khor ba/ nyon mongs pas rab tu dkrugs pa'i sems dang
44b2(phal chen): ldan pa| 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal chen po nyams su myong bar gyur pa/ 'khor ba na phongs pa'i sdug bsngal gyis rab tu gzir ba/ sangs rgyas blta ba las phyir phyogs
44b3(phal chen): par gyur pa thams cad gzigs nas thugs rje chen po'i thugs skyes par gyur to/ /sems can thams cad kyi don du 'gro ba thams cad la yo byad dang rin po ches yongs
44b4(phal chen): su bsdu zhing yongs su sdud pa'i thugs dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i yo byad yongs su sgrub pa'i thugs dang / dngos po thams cad la chags pa mi mnga' ba'i
44b5(phal chen): thugs dang / yul thams cad la ye rngam pa mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang / dga' ba thams cad la chags pa mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang / longs spyod thams cad la yongs
44b6(phal chen): su ma zhen pa'i thugs dang / sbyin pa thams cad la rnam par smin pa la re ba med pa'i thugs dang / 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad la bzhed pa mi mnga' ba'i
44b7(phal chen): thugs dang / rgyu dang rkyen la ma rmongs pa'i thugs dang / legs par btsal ba'i chos la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mkhyen pa'i thugs dang / sems can thams cad kyi
45a1(phal chen): don la gzhol bar bya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i thugs yang dag par skyes par gyur to/ /de de ltar chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la yang dag par
45a2(phal chen): zhugs pa'i thugs dang ldan pa/ sems can gyi khams thams cad du byams pa chen pos snyoms par zhugs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad thugs rje chen po'i sprin gyis rgyas
45a3(phal chen): par dgang ba'i sbyor ba mnga' ba/ sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad kun nas khebs pa'i chos kyi gdugs chen po'i dkyil 'khor mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad
45a4(phal chen): kyi nyon mongs pa'i ri rnam par 'joms pa'i ye shes rdo rje'i mtshon cha mnga' ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bde ba yongs su sgrub pas dgyes pa'i shugs rnam par 'phel ba'i
45a5(phal chen): thugs mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad la bde ba phul du phyin par mngon par sgrub pa'i smon lam gyi thugs mnga' ba/ bsam pa dang smon pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems
45a6(phal chen): can thams cad la nor gyi char rab tu dbab pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong zhing snyoms par sbyor ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ 'phags pa'i
45a7(phal chen): nor gyis sems can thams cad tshim par mdzad pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ stobs bcu'i ye shes rin po che phul du dri ma med pa thob par mdzad pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ byang
45b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa chen po'i stobs dang shugs rab tu brnyes pa de/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyi sprin chen pos sems can gyi
45b2(phal chen): khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad rgyas par bkang ste sems can thams cad la mngon par gyur par bzhugs shing sbyin pa'i
45b3(phal chen): dmigs pa thams cad kyi sprin gyi char chen po rnam pa thams cad du dbab pa dang / rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi sprin chen po'i char mngon par 'bebs pa mdzad de/ 'di ltar
45b4(phal chen): sems can thams cad so so'i tshul dang ji ltar mthun pas longs spyod par bya ba'i phyir dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa mtha' yas pa dang / yo byad rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pa la
45b5(phal chen): spyad par bya ba dang / sbyin pa rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis yongs su bsdu ba'i tshul dang / dngos po yongs su gtang ba rnam pa du ma la yongs su spyad pa dang / yo byad kyi rnam
45b6(phal chen): pa dang / rgyan gyi 'du byed brjod du med pa dang / sbyin pa'i tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs mtshan nyid sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ sems can rnams bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su
45b7(phal chen): tshim par bya ba'i sbyin pa'i tshul mtha' yas pa thugs su chud pas sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su tshim par bya ba/ mngon par bsgrubs pa'i dngos po
46a1(phal chen): thams cad gtang ba dang / yongs su gtang ba dang / sbyin pa bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal rgyun mi 'chad pa las yongs su
46a2(phal chen): bskyab pa'i tshul du bya ba rnams sems can thams cad la lan la re ba mi mnga' ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa nyid du 'byung ba'i thugs mnga' bas 'gro ba
46a3(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems rin po che yongs su sbyong ba mdzad cing / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtsho gcig tu gyur pa las byung ba'i yongs su bsdu ba'i tshul
46a4(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yo byad kyi char dbab pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i shugs rnam par
46a5(phal chen): 'phel bar mdzad pas thugs kyi skad cig re re la sems can ma lus pa thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rnam
46a6(phal chen): par dag par bya ba'i phyir mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re zhing gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ma lus pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar
46a7(phal chen): nyon mongs pa med cing bla na med pa'i rgyan rnam par dag pas rnam par klubs shing rab tu brgyan pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la chos kyi
46b1(phal chen): tshul rgya mtsho ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang bar rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la nam mkha'i dbyings kyi gtos ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par dgang
46b2(phal chen): ba'i ye shes kyi tshul yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la sems can dang dus ma lus pa thams cad la 'jug pa'i ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag par bya
46b3(phal chen): ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad rnam par 'dul ba'i ye shes kyi tshul snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la dus ma
46b4(phal chen): lus pa thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi byin gyi rlabs la mkhas
46b5(phal chen): pa ma lus par yongs su bstan pas 'gro ba thams cad la phan thogs par bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa'i grangs su bya ba'i rgyud
46b6(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byams klas
46b7(phal chen): pa sna tshogs brjod du yod pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rnam par gnas pa sna tshogs kyis mtshams rnam par 'dul ba/ gzhi sna tshogs dang / lhun du mar brjod du
47a1(phal chen): yod pa/ rnam par phye ba sna tshogs kyi bskal pa rnam pa tha dad pa bstan du yod pa/ kun nas nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa dang / rnam par dag
47a2(phal chen): cing kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / gcig tu yongs su dag pa dang / gcig tu kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / che ba dang / yangs pa dang / tshad med pa dang / dog pa dang / phra ba dang /
47a3(phal chen): rgya che ba dang / gzhi mnyam pa dang snrel zhi dang / spyi'u tshugs dang / phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su mngon par bltas pa dang / phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs su yongs su
47a4(phal chen): gzhol ba/ sgo sna tshogs nas bstan cing sgo mtha' yas pa'i dbyibs rnam pa sna tshogs su 'dug pa'i rnam par phye ba sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
47a5(phal chen): thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyod de/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa yongs su mnan nas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul
47a6(phal chen): pas rgyas par dgang bar bya ba dang / thugs kyi skad cig re re la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las ma lus pa thams cad sems can pha rol gyi sems dang bsam
47a7(phal chen): pas rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad la thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar mdzad de/ mngon par sgrub
47b1(phal chen): pa mdzad par gyur pas mngon par shes so/ /rjes su dran no/ /rigs kyi bu/ de ltar bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad sngon byang chub sems dpa'i
47b2(phal chen): spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe 'jig rten gnas pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dang bral ba/ sems can byas pa drin du mi gzo bas yongs su gang ba/ mi shes pa'i mun pas
47b3(phal chen): chod pa| bdag tu bya ba dang / bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ ma rig pa'i mun pa rab rib kyis bsgribs pa/ tshul bzhin ma yin par rnam par rtog pa la zhugs
47b4(phal chen): pa| lta ba thibs po bas dgon par mgo brlags pa/ rgyu dang 'bras bu la mgo rmongs pa/ nyon mongs pa dang las kyi dbang du gyur pa/ 'khor ba'i mya ngam chen po'i sdug bsngal
47b5(phal chen): gyi sa'i 'og tu lhung ba/ phongs pa'i sdug bsngal sna tshogs nyams su myong bar gyur pa rnams la thugs rje chen po bskyed de/ pha rol tu phyin pa sbyang ba'i sprin chen po
47b6(phal chen): mngon par bsgrubs te dge ba'i rtsa ba la brten par gnas pa/ yongs su bsngags pa dang sems can thams cad kyi 'khor ba'i phongs pa'i sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog pa
47b7(phal chen): dang / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs chen po la mngon par mos par bya ba dang / rgyu'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyogs mngon par bstan pa dang / las dang chos su mi 'gal
48a1(phal chen): ba'i phyogs rab tu brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su bsdu ba'i phyogs snang bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad
48a2(phal chen): kyi mos pa'i phyogs rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi zhing yongs su sgrub pa'i phyogs legs par bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams
48a3(phal chen): cad kyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyogs kyi rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa'i phyogs yongs su gzung ba dang / mi dge ba'i chos thams cad
48a4(phal chen): kyi phyogs rnam par bzlog pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs kyi phyogs yongs su brjod pa mdzad de/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i sprin chen pos sems can gyi khams
48a5(phal chen): t hams cad rgyas par bkang ste mngon par bsgrubs nas bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can tshim par 'gyur bar chos kyis shin tu bsdu ba la sems can rab tu
48a6(phal chen): dgod par mdzad do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs la yang dag par bskul to/ /byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa chen po la rab tu btsud do/ /'phags
48a7(phal chen): pa'i nor thams cad rab tu thob par bya bas nye bar bstan to/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'dun pa'i shugs kyis sems can rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya mtsho rnam par
48b1(phal chen): 'phags par mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par 'phrul pa'i sgor yang de dag rab tu btsud de/ phung po shin tu zhi ba'i bde bas yongs su bsdu ba bsdus te/ de bzhin
48b2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i bdag nyid che ba la mngon du mos par byas nas byang chub sems dpas yongs su bzung ba'i ye shes la rab tu bkod do/ /nor bzang gis smras pa/ 'phags ma
48b3(phal chen): khyod bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas ji srid cig lags/ smras pa/ rigs kyi bu/ gnas 'di ni/ yid ches par dka' ba ste/ shes
48b4(phal chen): par dka' ba'o/ /mos par dka' ba'o/ /'jug par dka' ba'o/ /brjod par dka' ba'o/ /khong du chud par dka' ba ste/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang / nyan thos dang rang
48b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang khong du chud par mi nus so/ /gzhan du na de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bzung ba ma
48b6(phal chen): gtogs te/ gnas 'di ni/ sems can 'khor ba'i bde ba thams cad la mngon par 'dod pa med pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba la lhag par dmigs pa/ sems
48b7(phal chen): can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i nan tan la mngon par mos pa/
49a1(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin nges par rtogs pa/ nam mkha'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ mos pa yangs pa'i lam gyis rnam par dag pa/
49a2(phal chen): 'khor ba'i rgyun las phyir phyogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes rgya mtsho la mngon par mos pa/ chos kyi grong khyer du 'gro bar gcig tu chad pa/
49a3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul yongs su gnon pa'i brtson 'grus can/ sangs rgyas kyi sa'i rgyud rnam par gnon pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs yongs su rdzogs
49a4(phal chen): par bya ba la mngon par mos pa/ stobs bcu rab tu thob par bya ba'i mthar thug pa rnams kyis bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs yangs pas nye bar bsten pa'i
49a5(phal chen): sems dang / bsam pa rnam par dag pa dang ma zhum pa/ nyon mongs pa med pa dang ma yo ba dang / ma nyams pa dang / ma 'chums pa dang / mun pa med pa'i sems dang /
49a6(phal chen): ye shes kyi snang ba kun tu snang bas snang bar gyur pa'i sems dang / sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde bar bya bar shin tu 'dun pa'i sems dang / bdud kyi
49a7(phal chen): 'khor dang nyon mongs pa thams cad kyis mi thub pa'i sems dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi ye shes thob par bya bar skabs phye ba'i sems kyis kyang khong du
49b1(phal chen): chud pa dang / 'jug pa dang / yid ches par bya ba dang / gzung ba dang / rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'am/ shes par bya ba mi nus so/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ gnas
49b2(phal chen): 'di ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi yul te/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis yongs su ma non na/ sems can gzhan thams cad kyis lta ci zhig smos/
49b3(phal chen): 'on kyang sems can cang shes rnams kyi bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba la spyod pa'i sems can rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam
49b4(phal chen): pa dbang du 'gyur bar bya ba dang / khyod kyis bsam pa thag pa nas yongs su dris pa'i lung bstan pa'i chos nyid rab tu 'byung ba thob par bya ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs
49b5(phal chen): pa'i byin gyis bstan to/ /de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo shing thams cad kyi me tog rgyas pas bde bar gnas pas de'i tshe don de nyid brnan te bstan pa'i phyir dus gsum du
49b6(phal chen): byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la rnam par bltas te tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /sangs rgyas sras po khyod kyis gang dris pa/ /de ni bsam yas zab
49b7(phal chen): mo sangs rgyas yul/ /bsam yas zhing gi rdul phran rab snyed kyi/ /bskal pa mang pos de kun brjod mi nus/ /sems can 'dod pa'i sems ldan sdang ba dang / /de bzhin
50a1(phal chen): gti mug mun pas bsgribs pa dang / /'chab dang dregs pas bsam pa nyams gyur pas/ /rgyal ba'i chos nyid zhi ba shes mi nus/ /phrag dog
50a2(phal chen): 'jungs pa'i dbang gi rjes 'brang dang / /g.yo sgyus bsam pa rnyog par gyur pa dang / /nyon mongs las kyi sgrib pas bsgribs pa yis/ /sangs rgyas yul 'di shes
50a3(phal chen): par mi nus so/ /phung po khams dang skye mched gnas pa dang / /'jig tshogs mang la gnas par gyur pa dang / /lta sems 'du shes phyin ci log gyur pas/ /zhi ba'i
50a4(phal chen): sa 'di shes par mi nus so/ /rgyal ba'i yul ni shes dka' zhi ba ste/ /rang bzhin dri med rnam par rtog pa med/ /srid par brten cing 'khor la chags pa yis/ /
50a5(phal chen): chos 'di yang dag shes par mi nus so/ /sangs rgyas rigs su rigs ldan gang skyes pa/ /de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis byin brlabs shing / /chos kyi rgyal po'i
50a6(phal chen): gdung rabs yongs 'dzin pa/ /drang srong de dag yul ni 'di yin no/ /dkar chos rgya mtshos mi ngoms sems ldan zhing / /gang rnams dge ba'i bshes kyis yongs
50a7(phal chen): bzung ste/ /thub pa'i stobs la dmigs pa'i sems sprin can/ /de dag 'di thos bzod pa thob par 'gyur/ /gang rnams bsam pa dri med rnams rtog med/ /bar snang
50b1(phal chen): mkha' bzhin phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su/ /mun pa rnam bsal blo gros sgron ma'i sprin/ /dri med de dag spyod yul 'di yin no/ /snying rje'i bsam pas 'gro ba rgya mtsho rnams/ /
50b2(phal chen): dus gsum byung ba gang rnams rgyas byed cing / /sems can ma lus rjes 'brang byams pa can/ /de dag rgyal ba'i tshul 'dir 'jug par 'gyur/ /gang rnams 'dzin med dga'
50b3(phal chen): ba'i sems ldan zhing / /rtag par bdog pa thams cad sbyin brtson la/ /sems can kun la mnyam par zhugs gyur pa/ /chags med de dag spyod yul sa 'di yin/ /nyon mongs
50b4(phal chen): med sems bskyod med spyod ldan zhing / /gang rnams 'gyod pa rnams bsal la sems ldan te/ /sangs rgyas gdams ngag nan tan byed ldan pa/ /dri med de dag spyod yul 'di
50b5(phal chen): yin no| |gang rnams mi sgul sems ldan mi bskyod sems/ /chos kyi rang bzhin rtogs pa'i sems ldan zhing / /las kyi rgya mtshor mi 'gal sems ldan pa/ /mi bzad de
50b6(phal chen): dag rnam thar 'di yin no/ /gang rnams mi skyo'i sems dang mi ldog sems/ /brtson 'grus mthu dang rtsal du ldan pa rnams/ /thams cad mkhyen tshogs brtson 'grus
50b7(phal chen): mtha' yas pa/ /brtul zhugs bzang ldan de dag yul 'di yin/ /zhi ba'i sems ldan mnyam par bzhag pa gang / /shin tu zhir gyur rim dang bral ba rnams/ /kun
51a1(phal chen): mkhyen bsam gtan yan lag mchor spyod pa/ /rab tu zhi ba de dag tshul 'di yin/ /gang rnams chags pa kun las sems grol zhing / /
51a2(phal chen): chos kyi rang bzhin khong du chud sems can/ /rgyal ba'i chos dbyings rtogs par khong chud pa/ /shes rab sgron ma de dag tshul 'di yin/ /sems can rang bzhin rtogs
51a3(phal chen): sems ldan gyur cing / /gang rnams srid pa'i mtsho la chags med sems/ /sems can sems la gzugs brnyan zla 'char ba/ /lam mkhan de dag rnam thar 'di
51a4(phal chen): yin no| |dus gsum byung ba'i rgyal ba rgya mtsho rnams/ /smon lam gang chen mtsho rgyud skyes pa yi/ /zhing rnams kun tu phyi ma'i mthar spyod pa/ /kun tu bzang po de
51a5(phal chen): dag tshul 'di yin/ /gang rnams chos dbyings tshul rnams rgya mtsho yis/ /'gro ba rgya mtsho 'du dang 'jig pa yi/ /bskal par bcas pa khong du chud pa rnams/ /rtog
51a6(phal chen): med de dag rnam thar 'di yin no/ /zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran thams cad la/ /sangs rgyas grangs med shing rgyal drung bzhugs shing / /byang chub 'tshang rgya 'gro 'dul
51a7(phal chen): mthong ba yi/ /chags med dmigs can de dag tshul 'di yin/ /khyod ni bskal pa rgya mtsho rgya chen du/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po bsnyen bkur te/ /chos
51b1(phal chen): 'dod chos tshol mi skyo 'dir phyin pas/ /thos nas de ni yongs su gzung bar nus/ /khyod kyi bsam pa yongs su sbyang ba'i phyir/ /bde gshegs byin rlabs bsam gyis
51b2(phal chen): mi khyab pas/ /rnam par snang mdzad tshad med yul 'di yang / /kho mo'i tshig las chags pa med par 'byung / /rigs kyi bu/ sngon byung ba'i dus bskal pa 'jig rten gyi
51b3(phal chen): khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol de'i yang pha snga zhig tu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba byung ste/ rigs kyi bu/
51b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba der de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes ri bo'i 'od chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzi brjid rgyal po zhes
51b5(phal chen): bya ba byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi ri bo'i 'od chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i gzi brjid rgyal po de/ sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe 'jig
51b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser rin po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa dang ri rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byams
51b7(phal chen): klas pa bstan du yod pa dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud re re zhing yang bskal pa'i grangs shin tu bstan pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang
52a1(phal chen): ldan pa| bskal pa re re zhing yang bskal pa bar ma shin tu bstan pa du ma dang ldan pa/ bskal pa bar ma re re zhing yang 'jig rten gyi khams rnam
52a2(phal chen): pa tha dad du bya ba bstan pa du ma dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba dang / rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs bstan du yod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa byung ba re re zhing yang
52a3(phal chen): mdo sde yang dag par bstan pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod du yod pa/ mdo sde re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i lung bstan pa 'jig rten gyi
52a4(phal chen): khams brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bstan du yod pa/ sems can 'dul ba mtha' dang dbus med pa shin tu bstan pa tha dad pa'i tshul gyis bsgrubs pa/
52a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul sna tshogs kyis rnam par 'dul ba dang ldan pa yongs su sbyangs te/ rigs kyi bu/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gser
52a6(phal chen): r in po che'i ri spos rnam par snang ba der 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud phyogs kun tu mngon par bltas pa'i sgo rgyal mtshan gyis rnam par brgyan pa zhes bya ba
52a7(phal chen): byung ste| rigs kyi bu/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud phyogs kun tu sgo mngon par bltas pa rgyal mtshan gyis rnam par brgyan pa der 'jig rten gyi khams rin
52b1(phal chen): po che thams cad kyi mdog kun tu snang ba'i dpal yon bya ba 'jig rten gyi khams kyi gzhi dang / mtshams kyi rgyan rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
52b2(phal chen): kyi snying po byang chub rab tu snang ba las byas pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog rgya mtsho la gnas pa/ lhun rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sprul
52b3(phal chen): pa'i gzugs brnyan rab tu ston pa las bsgrubs pa/ lha'i grong khyer gyi dbyibs su 'dug pa/ rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa byang bar gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi
52b4(phal chen): khams der gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung bar gyur to/ /gling bzhi pa'i ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag gi gling bzhi pa
52b5(phal chen): dbu ma rin po che sna tshogs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba byung ste/ gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna tshogs kyi rtse mo'i rgyal mtshan der gling mchu zhang du
