74b4(phal chen): 'byung ba'i smon lam dang / spyod pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir 'byung ba gcig gi 'du shes rab tu thob par gyur to/ /dge ba'i chos yongs su bsags pa thams
74b5(phal chen): cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho'i 'byung gnas kyi 'du shes rab tu thob bo/ /sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu thams cad
74b6(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes la brtson 'grus kyi shugs yongs su 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i chos yongs su ma rdzogs pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang / yang dag
74b7(phal chen): par 'phel bar byed pa dang / yongs su skyong ba'i 'du shes rab tu thob par gyur to/ /sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir
75a1(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i 'du shes rab tu thob par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi chos la dbang bsgyur
75a2(phal chen): bar rab tu gnas par bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la don thams cad yongs su sgrub pa'i 'du shes rab tu thob ste/ 'du shes rnam par dag pa bcu
75a3(phal chen): po de dag rab tu thob par gyur to/ /de dag thob pas mtshan mo'i lha mo 'gro ba thams cad srung ba'i smon lam la brtson pa'i 'od snang ba las byang chub sems
75a4(phal chen): dpa' dang skal pa mthun pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed thob par gyur te/ 'di ltar phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dus gsum
75a5(phal chen): rjes su dran pa'i tshul la dran pa'i skal ba mnyam pa dang / chos rgya mtsho'i tshul thams cad tha ma dad par khong du chud par bya ba la blo gros kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang /
75a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor rigs pas rjes su shes par bya ba'i bye brag dang / tshul tha dad par mkhas pa la rig pa'i
75a7(phal chen): skal pa mnyam pa dang / blo nam mkha' dang mnyam pas dus gsum thams cad kyi tshul rgya mtsho snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir blo'i skal pa mnyam pa dang /
75b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho shes pa'i snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir dbang po rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / rnam pa thams cad du sems
75b2(phal chen): c an yongs su bsdu ba'i rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi yon tan la nan tan du bya ba'i rgyan gyis lam khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir sems
75b3(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir spyod yul gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / thams
75b4(phal chen): cad mkhyen pa'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i lam snang ba rnam pa thams cad rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad
75b5(phal chen): kyi rang bzhin shes shing khong du chud pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir don khong du chud pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la chos la rnam par spyod pa'i
75b6(phal chen): skal pa mnyam pa dang / sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par gtor ba'i phyir mi 'jigs pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'gro ba rnams la rnam pa tha dad
75b7(phal chen): p ar yongs su bstan pa'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rnam par bris pa'i lus rnam par dag pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir gzugs kyi lus rnam par dag pa'i skal pa
76a1(phal chen): mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i stobs yongs su rdzogs pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dmigs pa rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir
76a2(phal chen): stobs kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems dang bsam pa'i nam mkha' yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir mi 'jigs pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / bskal pa thams
76a3(phal chen): cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pas mi skyo ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir btson 'grus kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad la sgrib pa med

76a5(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir zil gyis mi non pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mngon par dga' bar bya ba'i tshigs yongs su dag par bya ba'i
76a6(phal chen): phyir ma zhum mi dma' ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgra rab tu bsgrag pa'i phyir dbyangs kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / 'gro ba
76a7(phal chen): thams cad kyi tshig rnam par dmigs pa'i tha snyad dang / tshul rgya mtsho la dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
76b1(phal chen): pa'i gdams ngag gi yon tan khong du chud pa rnam par dag par bya ba la yon tan rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / kha na ma tho ba med pa'i las rnam par smin
76b2(phal chen): pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir chos dang las kyi rgyud du mi 'gal ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas byung ba thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i
76b3(phal chen): phyir mchod sbyin gyi chos bzang po la rab tu gnas pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul dang ye shes la yang dag par gnas par bya
76b4(phal chen): ba'i phyir tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnams par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / byams pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyis skad cig re re la sems can rgya mtsho thams cad du rgyas par dgang
76b5(phal chen): bar bya ba'i phyir byams pa chen po'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa'i phyir snying rje
76b6(phal chen): chen po'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par byed pa'i thabs kyi rgyud du skal pa mnyam par bya ba'i phyir lus
76b7(phal chen): kyi las kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad brjod cing smos pa la ngag gi las rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems la
77a1(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dmigs pa nye bar bsgrub pa'i phyir yid kyi las kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad la
77a2(phal chen): rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas 'byung brgya mtsho thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
77a3(phal chen): spyan sngar 'gro ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba gdab pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de
77a4(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la dus ma lus par mchod pa thams cad kyis rim gro bya ba'i phyir mchod pas rim gror bya ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems
77a5(phal chen): can gyi khams thams cad du sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang gdul ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi tshul thams cad la snang ba rab tu thob pa'i
77a6(phal chen): skal pa mnyam pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la ting nge 'dzin rab tu thob pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing rgya mtsho thams cad
77a7(phal chen): du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang rnam par 'phrul pas rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir kun tu rgyas par dgang ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
77b1(phal chen): thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i tshul rgya mtsho la byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par spyod pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pa la
77b2(phal chen): 'khor gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad shin tu phra bar 'jug pa la 'jug pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing shin tu yangs pa
77b3(phal chen): thams cad du sems rnam par phye ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa rnam pa tha dad pa khong du chud par bya ba la khong du chud
77b4(phal chen): pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rnam par phye ba ye shes mtha' yas pas rnam par dmigs par bya ba la tshul 'byams
77b5(phal chen): klas pas kun tu rgyas par dgang ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / phyogs thams cad
77b6(phal chen): rgyas par dgang bar yang dag par gzhol ba thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog par bya ba'i phyir mi ldog pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
77b7(phal chen): snying po byang chub tu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir mun pa rnam par sel ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas
78a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshor rjes su phyin pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i de bzhin
78a2(phal chen): gshegs pa mchod cing rim gro bya ba'i sbyor ba la sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad lus kyi dra bas rgyas par dgang ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi tshul rgya
78a3(phal chen): mtsho rjes su rgyu ba de dang de dag la ye shes mngon sum gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / rjes su mthun pa'i chos kyi tshul thams cad mngon du bya ba'i sbyor ba la nan tan
78a4(phal chen): gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi mos pa shin tu shas che ba'i brtsams pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir btsal ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / lus dang ngag
78a5(phal chen): dang yid kyi las kyis sangs rgyas kyi yon tan gyi rgyan yongs su sgrub pa la rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / nyam nga ba'i rtog pa med pa'i sems kyi
78a6(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyis chos thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir yid kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi tshogs
78a7(phal chen): yang dag par brtsams pa mthar phyin par bya ba'i sbyor ba la brtson 'grus brtsams pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad yongs
78b1(phal chen): su rdzogs par bya ba la spyod pa'i rgyan gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad kyi mtshan ma khong du chud par bya ba la chags pa med par rnam par spyad pa'i skal pa
78b2(phal chen): mnyam pa dang / chos la rnam par spyod pa'i ye shes kyis rnam par 'phrul pa de dang de dag tu thabs mkhas pa'i tshul gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / bsam pa ji lta ba
78b3(phal chen): bzhin du sems can rnams la yul bstan pas yang dag par bskul ba'i phyir skye mched rnam par dag pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos thams cad sgom pa dang /
78b4(phal chen): rnam par sgom pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo rab tu thob par bya ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams
78b5(phal chen): cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis rab tu thob par bya ba las yongs su gnan pa'i skal pa

79a1(phal chen): 'phrin las mtshan nyid sna tshogs la ting nge 'dzin rnam par dgod pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / rjes su dran pa'i dmigs pa'i tshul rgya mtsho
79a2(phal chen): thams cad la rjes su dran pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bya ba la phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par zhe non pa la byang chub sems
79a3(phal chen): dpas spyad pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes tshad med pa la mos shing dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir mos pa'i skal

79a5(phal chen): phyir phyir mi zlog pa'i ye shes kyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su sbyin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i dus su skye ba'i skal pa dang mnyam
79a6(phal chen): pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshul gyi sgo la rnam par spyod pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul gyis khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba'i yul la rab
79a7(phal chen): tu 'jug par bya ba'i phyir yul gyi skal pa mnyam pa dang / gzhi thams cad yongs su chom pa'i sems su bya ba'i phyir gzhi med pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang /
79b1(phal chen): chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos bstan pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs rang gi lus kyis yang

79b5(phal chen): kyi 'khor lo'i dgongs pa khong du chud par bya ba'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings lta bu'i chos kyi tshul thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir chos zab mo

80a1(phal chen): bstan pa'i phyir rab tu bskyod pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / mthong ba dang / thos pa dang / rjes su dran pas sems can gdul ba'i phyir don yod
80a2(phal chen): par spyad pa'i skal pa mnyam pa dang / smon lam rgya mtsho'i tshul thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas stobs bcu'i ye shes rjes su 'tshang rgya bar bya ba'i phyir 'byung ba'i

80b2(phal chen): te btud nas de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /de ni bdag gi sems la bdag dgongs te/ /byang chub mos pa mi ldog shin tu brtan/ /khyod kyi thugs

80b7(phal chen): ltung ba'i lam ni rnam par bzlog / mtho ris shul gtsang dam pa yongs su bstan/ /bde gshegs ma lus bzhud cing rjes bzhud pa'i/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i shul
81a1(phal chen): kyang khyod kyis bstan/ /dpe med rmad du byung mang khyod la bdag /'byung ba'i 'du shes dam pa nye bar skyes/ /nam mkha' lta bur dri med tshad

81b7(phal chen): kyi rang bzhin mnyam pa nyid khong du chud do/ /chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid la zhugs nas gnas med pa'i chos la brten te 'jig rten thams cad las 'phags par
82a1(phal chen): gyur to| |chos rnams kyi gzugs shin tu rnam par phye ba la zhugs te mi 'dra ba med pa'i kha dog dang / sna tshogs med pa'i kha dog dang / rnam pa
82a2(phal chen): tha dad pa med pa'i kha dog dang / mi rtog pa'i kha dog dang / mi sngo ba'i kha dog dang / mi ser ba'i kha dog dang / mi dmar ba'i kha dog dang / mi dkar ba'i kha dog dang / mi mthun pa med pa dang /

111b5(phal chen): snang ba'i 'od kyi snying po zhes bya ba'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba drug pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi rgyud du 'byung ba'i snying po
111b6(phal chen): zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyud du skyes pa yin/ tshul gyi sgo thams
111b7(phal chen): cad la shin tu grub pa yin/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi smon lam chen po la rnam par dag pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
112a1(phal chen): cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba la rang bzhin gcig pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bar gyur pa yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang lus gcig tu gyur pa yin/ chos dkar pos 'jig
112a2(phal chen): rten gzhan du 'gro ba yin/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs yongs su bstan pa'i ting nge 'dzin la bdag nyid che ba'i chos kyis rnam par spyod pa yin/ dus la ji ltar 'bab pa bzhin du
112a3(phal chen): sems can rnam par dag par bya ba'i chos la zhugs pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su dris pa la spobs pa rgyun mi 'chad pa yin te/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di ni/ byang chub sems
112a4(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba drug pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi rgyud du 'byung ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
112a5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba bdun pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs kyi 'od snang ba'i rgyan gyi snying po zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di la byang chub sems
112a6(phal chen): dpa' sangs rgyas kyi stobs la 'jug pa'i snang bas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro ba las phyir mi ldog go / byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rgya mtsho las phyir mi 'gyur ro/ /chos
112a7(phal chen): thams cad sgyu ma'i rnam pa ltar yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes par bya ba la gnas pas yongs su yi chad par mi 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten thams cad rmi lam lta bur rab tu rtogs
112b1(phal chen): par byed do/ /gzugs su rnam par dmigs pa'i gnas thams cad gzugs brnyan lta bur mngon par sgrub bo/ /mngon par shes pas rnam par 'phrul pa sprul pa lta bu la dbang rab tu thob
112b2(phal chen): par byed do/ /srid pa thams cad du skye ba grib ma lta bur gdod rab tu ston to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo sgra brnyan lta bur rab tu shes so/ /thabs kyi tshul
112b3(phal chen): don sna tshogs dang ldan pa la rab tu brtson pas chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rab tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa thob pa yin te/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
112b4(phal chen): rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba bdun pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs kyi 'od snang ba'i rgyan gyi snying po zhes bya'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de la byang chub sems dpa'
112b5(phal chen): rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba brgyad pa ye shes kyi sgo kun nas rnam par dpyad pas yongs su 'grub par 'byung ba'i snying po zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di la
112b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' gzhon nur gyur cing byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par dgod pa la rnam par gnas pa yin te/ de la gnas nas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ye shes kyi tshul la rnam
112b7(phal chen): par dpyod do/ /ye shes kyi tshul gyi sgo re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul tshad med par yongs su ston pas bskal pa tshad med par zad par 'gyur ro/ /byang chub sems dpa'i
113a1(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin thams cad la'ang pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pas dbang du 'gyur te/ sems kyi skad cig re re zhing sems kyi skad cig thams cad la yang phyogs
113a2(phal chen): bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi zhabs kyi drung du skyes te/ dmigs pa tha mi dad pas tha mi dad pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
113a3(phal chen): par 'jug go / tha mi dad pa'i chos rnams la tha dad pa'i ye shes kyi dbang yongs su ston to/ /dmigs pa brjod du med pa dag kyang bsgribs pa med pa'i dbyings yongs su non par
113a4(phal chen): byed do| |dmigs pa chung dus kyang mtha' yas pas brtan pa'i sa la yongs su 'jug go / chos nyid tshad med pa yang chung ba'am/ che bar khong du chud par byed do/ /'jig rten thams
113a5(phal chen): cad kyang rnam par dmigs pa dang / mnyam par rab tu rtogs par byed do/ /chos kyi dmigs pa thams cad dang / rnam par shes pa'i rgyud thams cad kyang sgom pas khong du chud par
113a6(phal chen): byed do| rigs kyi bu/ 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba brgyad pa ye shes kyi sgo kun nas rnam par dpyad pas yongs su 'grub pa 'byung
113a7(phal chen): ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'o/ /rigs kyi bu/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba dgu pa chos kyi dbyings sprul pas brgyan par byed pa'i snying po zhes bya ba
113b1(phal chen): gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems kyi skad cig thams cad la rgyan sna tshogs dang / rgyan du mar ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing byin gyis rlob ste/ sprul pa
113b2(phal chen): thams cad la mi 'jigs pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa thob pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa thams cad la shin tu mkhas par gyur pa yin/ chos kyi sprul pa la mi 'jigs pa rnam
113b3(phal chen): par dag pa yin/ chos kyi dbyings dam pa chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa yin/ bsam pa ji bzhin du sems can gyi lus rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i byin gyi rlabs
113b4(phal chen): la mkhas pa yin/ sems can gdul ba mkhas pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa yin/ spyod pa sna tshogs kyis mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su ston pa yin/ thams cad
113b5(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid kyi lam sgrib pa med pa mngon par sgrub pa la mkhas pa yin/ de'i rgyud kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la mkhas pa yongs su ston pa yin/ sems can mtha' dang dbus
113b6(phal chen): med pa gdul ba'i thabs mngon par sgrub pa la mkhas pa yin/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi ye shes dbyig tu bya ba'i mdzod dang ldan pas sems can gdul ba'i dus la bab na rtag
113b7(phal chen): tu sta gon du gnas pa yin te/ rigs kyi bu/ 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba dgu pa chos kyi sprul pas brgyan par byed pa'i snying po zhes bya
114a1(phal chen): ba'o| |rigs kyi bu/ de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba bcu pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yongs su gnon pa'i shugs
114a2(phal chen): drag po'i snying po zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang rang bzhin gcig pa'i yul la dbang bskur ba yin te/
114a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dab chags pa'i yul la rab tu 'jug pa yin/ sems can thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i shi 'pho ba dang / skye ba'i
114a4(phal chen): sems rgyun chags par 'byung ba'ang rab tu shes so/ /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ye shes 'dab chags pa'i yul yang rab tu shes so/ /'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang /
114a5(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba 'dab chags pa yang rab tu shes so/ /chos thams cad kyi rgyud 'dab chags pa la mkhas par bya ba yang rab tu shes
114a6(phal chen): so| |bskal pa 'jig pa dang 'du ba thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyang ming dang bcas/ sa tshigs dang bcas par 'dab chags par
114a7(phal chen): rab tu shes so/ /sems can tshul ji lta bur yongs su smin par byas pa dang / dus la gang du 'bab pa rnams la mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i rgyan dang / rnam par 'tshang rgya bas
114b1(phal chen): gdul bar bya ba yongs su bstan pa'i phyin gyi rlabs kyi ye shes kyang mngon par sgrub bo/ /sangs rgyas byung ba thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i drung du nye bar 'gro zhing chos kyi 'khor lo
114b2(phal chen): bskor ba la mkhas pa'i tshul 'dab chags pa yang sems can gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med pa gdul ba'i thabs mngon par sgrub pa la mkhas pas yongs su ston te/ rigs kyi bu/

114b4(phal chen): ni| byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i skye ba bcu rnams te/ de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams skye bar 'gyur ba'o/ /'byung bar 'gyur ba'o/ /yang dag
114b5(phal chen): par sgrub bar byed pa'o/ /yang dag par 'phel bar byed pa'o/ /rab tu rdzogs par byed pa'o/ /yongs su grub par byed pa'o/ /zhing ma lus pa thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir rgyan
114b6(phal chen): gcig gi lhab lhub la rgyan dang lhab lhub kyi rgyud rnam pa sna tshogs byin gyis rlob pa'o/ /sems can gyi khams gdul ba rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par
114b7(phal chen): byin gyis rlabs kyis rgyun chad pa med par byed pa'o/ /chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dmigs pa sna tshogs dang / shin tu bstan pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa sna tshogs du ma
115a1(phal chen): rnam pa tha dad pa dang / chos mtha' yas pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rgyun mngon par 'tshang rgya bar byed pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung
115a2(phal chen): ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' gtugs pa yongs su ston pa'o/ /sems can tshad med pa spyod pa rgya mtsho sna tshogs
115a3(phal chen): dang ldan pa yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bas yongs su 'dus pa rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongs su ston pa'o/ /sems can gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas
115a4(phal chen): 'byung ba dang mi 'bral bar byin gyis rlob pa'o/ /chos thams cad kyi sprin dbyangs kyi yan lag rgya mtsho brjod du med pas rnam par dag pa dmigs pa thams cad las rab tu 'byung
115a5(phal chen): ba rnam par dmigs par byed pa'o/ /tshad med par rnam par spyad pa la sgrib pa med par rtogs pas khong du chud pa rnams chos yid du 'ong ba'i rgyan thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub
115a6(phal chen): sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor bsam pa dang / mos pa gang dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can rnams la yongs su ston pa'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi sa tshad med pa'i rjes su song ba rnams
115a7(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad yongs su bsgrub pa'i don du chos kyi mdzod mtha' dang dbus med pa rab tu ston pa'o/ /de nas lum+bi ni'i nags tshal kyi lha mo gzi brjid kyi dkyil 'khor bzang
115b1(phal chen): p os dga' ba'i dpal gyis de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi don 'di nyid gsal bar brjod pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te tshong dpon gyi
115b2(phal chen): bu nor bzang la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa dri med rnyog pa med pa yis/ /gang rnams rgyal ba blta bas nam yang mi ngoms shing / /rgyal ba kun gyi phyi ma'i mtha' yi
115b3(phal chen): rgyan sprin la/ /smon pa'i mkhas pa de dag skye ba'i thog ma gnas/ /dus gsum byung ba'i 'jig rten ma lus kun bkang ste/ /zhing dang sems can de bzhin chos dang sangs rgyas rnams/ /

115b6(phal chen): ri rab brdo rje mtshungs brtan pas/ /thams cad mkhyen tshul rgya mtshor rnam par 'jug byed cing / /gang rnams snying rje chen po'i gang chen mtshor 'jug pa/ /de ni skyes bu khyu mchog rnams kyi

116a1(phal chen): bu chen po de dag skye ba lnga/ /chos kyi rang bzhin rab tu rtogs pas chags med sems/ /dus gsum dpe zla med pa'i sangs rgyas rigs byung zhing / /gang rnams

116a3(phal chen): lus kyis dgang byas shing / /sangs rgyas stobs rnams ma lus khong du chud rtogs pa/ /de ni mkhas pa rnams kyi skye ba bsam yas bdun/ /gang rnams ye shes rgya mtsho'i tshul
116a4(phal chen): la dbang ldan zhing / /thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo tshul rnam par dpyod byed la/ /ting nge 'dzin kun tshul gang chen mtsho la yongs 'jug pa/ /de ni de bzhin nyid rten rnams kyi skye ba brgyad/

116a6(phal chen): pa| |de ni grangs pa chen po rnams kyi skye ba dgu/ /gang rnams rgyal ba'i stobs rnams ji bzhin rab zhugs te/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i shugs drag yangs pa rnam spel cing / /

117a4(phal chen): gyur pa 'di ni/ sngon gyi ltas gnyis pa byung ba'o/ /yang lum+bi ni'i nags tshal 'di thams cad rin po che thams cad kyi shing dang / sA la dang / ta la'i phreng bas rnam par 'khrigs

117a6(phal chen): myu gu kun nas thon pa dang / phye ma thams cad kyi mdzod kun nas thon pa dang / rgyal mtshan thams cad kyi sprin dang na bun yongs su byung ba dang / spos kyi rin po che'i gzugs kyi
117a7(phal chen): shing drung kun nas 'khor te rgyan yongs su sbyangs par kun nas gnas par gyur pa 'di ni/ sngon gyi ltas bzhi pa byung ba'o/ /yang lum+bi ni'i nags tshal 'di thams cad lha rdzas kyi me

159a3(phal chen): la mkhas/ /'jig rten kun na bzo rnams ji snyed pa/ /ma lus de la 'di ni pha rol phyin/ /mda' gzhu'i tshul la'ang rnam pa brgyas su mkhas/ /'phong gi cho ga rnam pa rangs par
159a4(phal chen): rtogs| |dgra yid bzho zhing dbab pa kun la yang / /'di ni mchog tu pha rol phyin par gyur/ /lus rnams kun nas rin chen rnam dag pa'i/ /'od mchog 'khor gyis shin tu
159a5(phal chen): mdzes pa ste/ /sngon gyi legs pas shin tu sdug par brgyan/ /'di ni khyod kyi phyag rjed khyod la 'os/ /mi yi 'jig rten gnas rnams ji snyed pa/ /de dag gso ba'i tshul gyi cho ga
159a6(phal chen): 'tshal| |de dag ma lus thams cad zhir bgyi na'ang / /ma nor sman gyi cho gas gso la mkhas/ /dzam+bu'i rgyal mtshan skad rnams thams cad dang / /skye bo'i nges tshig ma lus bye

159b1(phal chen): rab tu zhugs/ /'jig rten glu gar rnam pa ji snyed pa/ /ma lus de rnams kun gyi tshul yang 'tshal/ /rol mo sil snyan dag gi thabs rnams dang / /bzhad gad rol mo'i tshul la rnam par
159b2(phal chen): mkhas| |chags dang ma chags mi rnams mngon 'tshal kyang / /khong khro chags par 'gyur ba ma mchis so/ /'jig rten bud med sgra rnams ji snyed pa/ /khyad par nang du de la ma lus
159b3(phal chen): 'tshal| |bud med skye bo'i skyon du bgyi ba rnams/ /grangs med de dag 'di la gcig ma mchis/ /thil gyis blta dang zur gyis blta ba dang / /yan lag bstabs dang yan lag rnams
159b4(phal chen): bstan dang / /shes nyen kun la mkhas pa'i mthar phyin te/ /khyod kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs par bgyid/ /'di ni phrag dog ser sna ma mchis te/ /'dod pa zhe dug mi ldang

160a1(phal chen): rten kun la sman par dga' ba ste/ /rlabs chen sems kyi yon tan kun gyis brgyan/ /mchis sam nyal lam mchi 'am 'greng yang rung / /smra'am

216a7(phal chen): pa'i 'od 'di shes par zad na/ kho bos byang chub sems dpa' rnam par thar pa tshad med pa thob pa rnams kyi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/
216b1(phal chen): song rigs kyi bu/ lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na grong khyer ri dwags gnas zhes bya ba yod de/ de na khyim bdag mi pham sde zhes bya ba 'dug gi/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang

217b5(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog / ldog par mi 'gyur zhe na/ bden pa'i tshig gi byin gyi rlabs des bdag gi dgos pa 'di dang 'di zhig grub par shog

218a1(phal chen): spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu/ lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na grong khyer yid bzang po'i sgo zhes bya ba yod
218a2(phal chen): de| de na khye'u dpal 'byung ba zhes bya ba dang / bu mo dpal gyi blo gros ma zhes bya ba gnyis shig 'khod kyi/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub

218a4(phal chen): ' dzin mchog gi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag byas nas bram ze zhi 'dzin mchog la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te yang dang yang bltas nas

218b5(phal chen): thams cad sgyu ma'i rnam par rgyu rkyen sgyu ma las byung bar mthong ngo / /las dang nyon mongs pa sgyu mar shes pas sems can thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par shes so/ /ma rig
218b6(phal chen): pa dang / srid pa dang / sred pa'i rgyu las byung bas 'gro ba thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par mthong ngo / /phan tshun gyi rkyen gyi rgyu las byung bas chos thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam
218b7(phal chen): par mthong ngo / /phyin ci log gi rgyu las byung bas khams gsum thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par mthong ngo / /yang dag pa ma yin pa'i rtog pa'i rgyus bskyed pas sems
219a1(phal chen): can thams cad kyi 'chi 'pho dang / 'byung ba dang / skye ba dang / rga shi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde ba dang
219a2(phal chen): 'khrug pa rnams kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par mthong ngo / /'du shes dang / sems dang / lta ba phyin ci log gi rgyu las dngos po med pa'i 'du shes kyis rmongs te byung bas zhing
219a3(phal chen): thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par mthong ngo / /ye shes kyi spong ba'i rgyu la brtags te bskyed pas nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyang sgyu ma'i rnam par

220a3(phal chen): ma dang / gnyen du gyur pa rnams yongs su smin par bya ba dang / der skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' skal pa mnyam pa rnams kyi theg pa chen po rab tu bstan par

223b5(phal chen): bdud rtsi'i tshogs tshad med pa yang dag par bsdu bar bya dgos so/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang tshad med pa 'da' bar bya dgos so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med
223b6(phal chen): pa mchod dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med par 'jug par bya dgos so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa tshad med pa yongs
223b7(phal chen): su gzung dgos so/ /sems can gyi gnod pa tshad med pa bzod par bya dgos so/ /mi khom pa dang / ngan song gi lam tshad med pa yongs su gcad dgos so/ /sems
224a1(phal chen): can gyi bde ba tshad med pa nye bar bsgrub dgos so/ /sems can bsdu ba tshad med pa bya dgos so/ /gzungs kyi sgo tshad med pa yongs su sbyang
224a2(phal chen): dgos so/ /smon lam gyi sgo tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa dgos so/ /byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po'i stobs tshad med pa yongs su bsgom dgos so/ /
224a3(phal chen): chos yongs su btsal ba la brtson par bya ba tshad med pa rgyun mi gcad par bya dgos so/ /nges par rtogs pa'i stobs tshad med pa'i rjes su 'jug dgos so/ /mngon
224a4(phal chen): par shes pa mngon du sgrub pa tshad med pa bskyed dgos so/ /rig pa dang / ye shes kyi snang ba tshad med pa rnam par dag par bya dgos so/ /sems can gyi rgyud

224a6(phal chen): skad rnam par phye ba tshad med pa yongs su shes par bya dgos so/ /sems can gyi sems rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pa khong du chud par bya dgos so/ /byang chub

224b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i rnam par spyod pa zab mo la rnam par blta dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i yul rtogs par dka' ba khong du chud par bya dgos so/ /byang chub sems
224b2(phal chen): dpa'i lam bgrod par dka' ba bgrod par bya dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i shugs sgrub par dka' ba yongs su gzung dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med
224b3(phal chen): par 'jug par dka' ba la 'jug par bya dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rnam pa sna tshogs khong du chud par bya dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul

224b7(phal chen): med pa yongs su sbyang dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpas chos kyi sgo dpag tu med pa yongs su dag par bya dgos so/ /byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi zhing

225a3(phal chen): so| |rigs kyi bu/ mdor na/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par byed pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa ni/ sems can thams cad dang mnyam par

341a1(phal chen): yang bdag gis der thob shog / der ni bdag gis lung bstan rab thob nas/ /sprul pa mang po bye ba phrag brgya yis/ /blo yi stobs kyis phyogs bcu rnams
341a2(phal chen): su yang / /sems can rnams la phan pa mang po bgyi/ /gang gis bzang po spyod pa ston pa yis/ /dge ba cung zad bdag gis ci bsags pa/ /des ni 'gro ba'i smon lam dge ba
341a3(phal chen): rnams| |skad cig gcig gis thams cad 'byor par shog / gang yang bzang po spyod pa bsngos pa yis/ /bsod nams mtha' yas dam pa thob pa des/ /'gro ba sdug bsngal chu
341a4(phal chen): bor bying ba rnams/ /'od dpag med pa'i gnas rab 'gro bar shog /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi nang
